msg:I just returned from Atour Hotel Changsha, and I can only describe this stay experience as "amazing". The hotel rooms are well designed and extremely comfortable, and each window is like a picture frame, framing the beautiful scenery of Changsha. It is particularly worth mentioning that due to the high-rise design of the hotel, guests can overlook the entire city of Changsha and even have a clear view of the river, which deeply shocked me.
As a frequent business traveler and a manager who once worked at Four Seasons Hotel, I know the value of quality service. Atour Hotel Changsha has shown a very high cost-effectiveness with its high-quality service and reasonable price. Here, I especially want to praise two employees: A Quan and Tiao Tiao Yu on the night shift. Although it was two o'clock in the morning, when I asked for an extra quilt, they not only did not refuse, but also quickly provided me with help. This professional and meticulous service attitude is rare even in some five-star hotels.
The service of Atour Hotel Changsha is not only reflected in the professionalism of the staff, but also in their enthusiasm and caring. Every employee serves the guests attentively, making people feel the warmth of home. In general, Changsha Atour Hotel is a highly recommended hotel. Whether it is a business trip or a leisure trip, it can provide you with an unforgettable stay experience.

name:A‚Äçm‚Äço‚Äçr‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äça‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçm‚Äçe‚Äçi
info:Guestroom - with View (2 beds)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Business travelers
info:19 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 19, 2024
msg:Facilities: The hotel facilities are quite new, equipped with a smart toilet lid, and the experience of the hotel front desk on the 48th floor is also quite magical. When I booked here before, I actually read other people's comments. Some people pointed out that the hotel's residential floors are all above the 49th floor. There are only two elevators, and the waiting time is relatively long, so I was quite worried about this problem when I checked in. But after my personal experience, the so-called two elevators are Atour's special elevators, and they will not stop between the 1st and 49th floors, so the waiting time is not very long. The time from the 1st floor to the 49th floor is 1 minute. I hope my comments can be used as a reference for those who stay later. One thing that is a little regrettable is the sound insulation. Atour's doors have always used heavier doors. Although they are safer, the sound insulation effect does not seem to be particularly good, and the door closing sound is louder. In Changsha, a city with rich nightlife, the laughter and door closing of people returning at night have a little effect on us, who are tired of going to bed early on business trips.

Hygiene: Atour's hygiene has always been pretty good. Every day, the room cleaning can be done in time to clean up the garbage in the room. However, there is one thing here. In fact, guests who stay longer do not necessarily need to replace toothpaste and shower caps all the time. The aunt can add new ones in the small drawer, but she does not need to help guests throw away the hanging shower caps and used toothpaste, which can avoid unnecessary waste.

Environment: The location of this hotel is very good. It is in the central area. It is not far from the Provincial Museum, May Day Square, Orange Island, and Yuelu Mountain. It is also close to the office, which is quite good. It is a bit regrettable that the windows of the twin room with a view are on both sides instead of in the middle. There is a solid wall in the middle, which does not feel like a view room.

Service: The service is as good as always, and it can respond to our needs quickly. Thumbs up!
In general, this hotel is still very cost-effective.
